using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report19EdgeDeathMapReportService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary<int, StrategyFitnessSnapshot> fitnessSnapshots,
        IReadOnlyCollection<int> allowedStrategyIds)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(allowedStrategyIds);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_19_EDGE_DEATH_MAP_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var selectedMarkets = result.SelectedMarkets?
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList()
            ?? new List<string>();

        var rejectionMap = result.MarketSelectionRejections?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key))
            .GroupBy(kv => kv.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToDictionary(
                g => g.Key,
                g => g.Last().Value ?? string.Empty,
                StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var candidateUniverse = selectedMarkets
            .Concat(rejectionMap.Keys)
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var canonicalDeployable = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key) && kv.Value > 0m)
            .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary<string, decimal>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var runnerCandidateMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key) && kv.Value > 0m)
            .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary<string, decimal>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        int rawCandidateCount = candidateUniverse.Count;
        int rejectedCount = rejectionMap.Count;
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount = selectedMarkets.Count;
        int deployableCount = canonicalDeployable.Count;
        decimal preservedCash = result.CashAllocationWeight;

        int totalStrategies = fitnessSnapshots.Count;
        int allowedStrategies = allowedStrategyIds.Count;
        int rejectedStrategies = Math.Max(0, totalStrategies - allowedStrategies);
        int scarcityOverrideCount = fitnessSnapshots.Values.Count(x =>
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x.GateReason) &&
            x.GateReason.Contains("SCARCITY_OVERRIDE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

        int lostInCanonicalNormalization = selectedMarkets.Count(x =>
            !canonicalDeployable.ContainsKey(x));

        var rejectionReasonCounts = BuildRejectionReasonCounts(rejectionMap);
        var strategyGateReasonCounts = BuildStrategyGateReasonCounts(fitnessSnapshots);
        string dominantKillZone = DetermineDominantKillZone(
            rejectionReasonCounts,
            strategyGateReasonCounts,
            selectedAfterWaveBCount,
            deployableCount,
            preservedCash);

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 19 — EDGE DEATH MAP");
        sb.AppendLine("==========================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Institutional funnel audit of where candidate breadth is dying.");
        sb.AppendLine("This report is designed to explain why final deployable alpha breadth is narrow.");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)              : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Raw Candidate Universe           : {rawCandidateCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected Before Final Deploy     : {rejectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected After Wave B            : {selectedAfterWaveBCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Count       : {runnerCandidateMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Count       : {deployableCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Preserved Cash Weight            : {preservedCash:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Strategies Evaluated       : {totalStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Allowed               : {allowedStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Rejected              : {rejectedStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Scarcity Override Count          : {scarcityOverrideCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Lost In Canonical Normalization  : {lostInCanonicalNormalization}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION A — CANDIDATE FUNNEL");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"1. Raw Candidate Universe             : {rawCandidateCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"2. Markets Rejected (reason present)  : {rejectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"3. Markets Selected After Wave B      : {selectedAfterWaveBCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"4. Runner Candidate Mix Count         : {runnerCandidateMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"5. Canonical Deployable Markets       : {deployableCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"6. Preserved Cash                     : {preservedCash:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION B — MARKET REJECTION REASON COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------------------");
        if (rejectionReasonCounts.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO MARKET REJECTION DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in rejectionReasonCounts.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-36} {kv.Value,6}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION C — STRATEGY GATE REASON COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------");
        if (strategyGateReasonCounts.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STRATEGY GATE DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in strategyGateReasonCounts.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-36} {kv.Value,6}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION D — NEAR MISS MARKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        WriteNearMissMarkets(sb, result, rejectionMap);
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION E — STRATEGY FITNESS SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------------");
        if (fitnessSnapshots.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO FITNESS SNAPSHOT DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("StrId | StrategyCode | Allowed | Trades | Exits | FitnessScore | PnL | GateReason");
            sb.AppendLine("------+--------------+---------+--------+-------+--------------+-----+-----------");
            foreach (var row in fitnessSnapshots.Values.OrderBy(x => x.StrategyId))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.StrategyId,5} | " +
                    $"{TrimTo(row.StrategyCode, 12),-12} | " +
                    $"{(row.Allowed ? "YES" : "NO "),-7} | " +
                    $"{row.Trades,6} | " +
                    $"{row.Exits,5} | " +
                    $"{row.FitnessScore,12:F4} | " +
                    $"{row.PnL,7:F2} | " +
                    $"{row.GateReason}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION F — FINAL DEPLOYABLE ALLOCATION");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------");
        if (canonicalDeployable.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE MARKETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in canonicalDeployable.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-24} {kv.Value,10:P2}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine($"CASH{' ',20} {preservedCash,10:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION G — BREADTH KILL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Kill Zone : {dominantKillZone}");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdictNarrative(
            dominantKillZone,
            rawCandidateCount,
            selectedAfterWaveBCount,
            deployableCount,
            preservedCash,
            scarcityOverrideCount,
            lostInCanonicalNormalization));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION H — OPERATOR INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("This report should be used before changing thresholds.");
        sb.AppendLine("Do not loosen gates blindly.");
        sb.AppendLine("First identify where breadth dies:");
        sb.AppendLine("1) market selection / Wave B");
        sb.AppendLine("2) strategy fitness gating");
        sb.AppendLine("3) canonical CIO deployment");
        sb.AppendLine("4) preserved-cash regime defense");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static Dictionary<string, int> BuildRejectionReasonCounts(
        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> rejectionMap)
    {
        var counts = new Dictionary<string, int>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var kv in rejectionMap)
        {
            string bucket = NormalizeMarketRejectionReason(kv.Value);
            if (counts.TryGetValue(bucket, out int current))
                counts[bucket] = current + 1;
            else
                counts[bucket] = 1;
        }

        return counts;
    }

    private static Dictionary<string, int> BuildStrategyGateReasonCounts(
        IReadOnlyDictionary<int, StrategyFitnessSnapshot> fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        var counts = new Dictionary<string, int>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var row in fitnessSnapshots.Values)
        {
            string reason = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(row.GateReason)
                ? (row.Allowed ? "ALLOWED" : "UNKNOWN")
                : row.GateReason.Trim();

            if (counts.TryGetValue(reason, out int current))
                counts[reason] = current + 1;
            else
                counts[reason] = 1;
        }

        return counts;
    }

    private static string NormalizeMarketRejectionReason(string? reason)
    {
        string value = reason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return "UNKNOWN";

        if (value.Contains("dispersion", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "DispersionGuard";

        if (value.Contains("per-symbol", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("per symbol", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("symbol cap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PerSymbolCap";

        if (value.Contains("top-n", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("top n", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "TopNOverflow";

        if (value.Contains("threshold", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("below", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("score", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "BelowMinScore";

        if (value.Contains("pre-trade", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("pretrade", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PreTradeSelection";

        if (value.Contains("duplicate", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "DuplicateFiltered";

        return value;
    }

    private static string DetermineDominantKillZone(
        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int> marketRejectionReasons,
        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int> strategyGateReasons,
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount,
        int deployableCount,
        decimal preservedCash)
    {
        int marketRejectTotal = marketRejectionReasons.Values.Sum();
        int strategyRejectTotal = strategyGateReasons
            .Where(kv => !kv.Key.Equals("ALLOWED", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                         !kv.Key.Contains("SCARCITY_OVERRIDE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .Sum(kv => kv.Value);

        if (selectedAfterWaveBCount <= 1 && marketRejectTotal >= strategyRejectTotal)
            return "WAVE_B_SELECTION";

        if (strategyRejectTotal > marketRejectTotal && strategyRejectTotal > 0)
            return "STRATEGY_FITNESS_GATING";

        if (deployableCount < selectedAfterWaveBCount)
            return "CANONICAL_CIO_DEPLOYMENT";

        if (preservedCash >= 0.50m)
            return "REGIME_CASH_PRESERVATION";

        return "MIXED_OR_UNCLEAR";
    }

    private static void WriteNearMissMarkets(
        StringBuilder sb,
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> rejectionMap)
    {
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL
            ?? new Dictionary<string, decimal>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var rows = rejectionMap
            .Select(kv => new
            {
                Market = kv.Key,
                Reason = kv.Value,
                PnL = symbolTfPnl.TryGetValue(kv.Key, out decimal pnl) ? pnl : 0m
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.PnL)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Market, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(10)
            .ToList();

        if (rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO NEAR MISS MARKET DATA");
            return;
        }

        sb.AppendLine("Market                    PnL         Reason");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------  ----------  --------------------------------");
        foreach (var row in rows)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{TrimTo(row.Market, 24),-24}  {row.PnL,10:F2}  {row.Reason}");
        }
    }

    private static string BuildVerdictNarrative(
        string dominantKillZone,
        int rawCandidateCount,
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount,
        int deployableCount,
        decimal preservedCash,
        int scarcityOverrideCount,
        int lostInCanonicalNormalization)
    {
        return dominantKillZone switch
        {
            "WAVE_B_SELECTION" =>
                $"Breadth is dying primarily before or during Wave B. " +
                $"Raw candidates = {rawCandidateCount}, selected after Wave B = {selectedAfterWaveBCount}. " +
                $"This suggests market-level selection pressure is the main bottleneck.",

            "STRATEGY_FITNESS_GATING" =>
                $"Breadth is dying primarily at strategy fitness gating. " +
                $"Markets are surviving far enough to be candidates, but too many strategy sleeves are rejected before robust deployment.",

            "CANONICAL_CIO_DEPLOYMENT" =>
                $"Breadth is dying between runner selection and final deployable CIO normalization. " +
                $"Selected after Wave B = {selectedAfterWaveBCount}, final deployable = {deployableCount}, " +
                $"lost in canonical normalization = {lostInCanonicalNormalization}.",

            "REGIME_CASH_PRESERVATION" =>
                $"The main visible constraint is defensive capital preservation. " +
                $"Preserved cash = {preservedCash:P2}. " +
                $"Scarcity override count = {scarcityOverrideCount}. " +
                $"The platform is choosing honesty over forced deployment.",

            _ =>
                $"No single bottleneck dominates cleanly. " +
                $"This run likely reflects mixed pressure across Wave B, strategy gating, and final deployable normalization."
        };
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }
}

using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class ReportPortalPublishService
{
    private const string PortalRootFolderName = "TQGA_REPORT_PORTAL";
    private const string SiteFolderName = "site";
    private const string RawFolderName = "raw";

    private static readonly LocalStaticSiteHost _localHost = new();

    public PublishPortalResult PublishLatestReports()
    {
        string reportDir = DataPaths.Reports;
        Directory.CreateDirectory(reportDir);

        string portalRoot = ResolvePortalRoot(reportDir);
        string siteDir = Path.Combine(portalRoot, SiteFolderName);
        string rawDir = Path.Combine(siteDir, RawFolderName);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(portalRoot);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(siteDir);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(rawDir);

        ClearDirectoryContents(siteDir, [RawFolderName]);
        ClearDirectoryContents(rawDir, []);

        List<string> allFiles = Directory
            .GetFiles(reportDir, "*.*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        List<PublishedReportEntry> entries = [];

        foreach (string filePath in allFiles)
        {
            string relativePath = Path.GetRelativePath(reportDir, filePath);
            string normalizedRelativePath = relativePath.Replace('\\', '/');
            string rawRelativePath = normalizedRelativePath;

            string rawOutputPath = Path.Combine(rawDir, relativePath);
            string? rawOutputFolder = Path.GetDirectoryName(rawOutputPath);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(rawOutputFolder))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(rawOutputFolder);

            File.Copy(filePath, rawOutputPath, overwrite: true);

            FileInfo info = new(filePath);
            bool isTextReport = info.Extension.Equals(".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            string? htmlPageFileName = null;

            if (isTextReport)
            {
                string htmlSafeName = BuildHtmlPageFileName(relativePath);
                string htmlPath = Path.Combine(siteDir, htmlSafeName);
                string content = ReadAllTextSafe(filePath);

                File.WriteAllText(
                    htmlPath,
                    BuildReportHtml(
                        displayName: relativePath,
                        sourcePath: filePath,
                        info: info,
                        content: content,
                        rawHref: BuildRawHref(rawRelativePath)),
                    Encoding.UTF8);

                htmlPageFileName = htmlSafeName;
            }

            entries.Add(new PublishedReportEntry
            {
                DisplayName = relativePath,
                SourcePath = filePath,
                RelativeRawPath = rawRelativePath,
                HtmlPageFileName = htmlPageFileName,
                IsTextReport = isTextReport,
                Modified = info.LastWriteTime,
                SizeBytes = info.Length
            });
        }

        string indexPath = Path.Combine(siteDir, "index.html");
        File.WriteAllText(
            indexPath,
            BuildIndexHtml(reportDir, siteDir, entries),
            Encoding.UTF8);

        string baseUrl = _localHost.Start(siteDir, 8787);
        string localWebUrl = baseUrl + "index.html";

        TryOpenInBrowser(localWebUrl);

        return new PublishPortalResult
        {
            Success = true,
            ReportDirectory = reportDir,
            PortalRootDirectory = portalRoot,
            SiteDirectory = siteDir,
            IndexFilePath = indexPath,
            ReportCount = entries.Count,
            LocalWebUrl = localWebUrl
        };
    }

    private static string ResolvePortalRoot(string reportDir)
    {
        DirectoryInfo? current = new(reportDir);

        while (current != null)
        {
            if (current.Name.Equals("D DATA BACKUP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return Path.Combine(current.FullName, PortalRootFolderName);

            current = current.Parent;
        }

        string reportParent = Directory.GetParent(reportDir)?.FullName ?? reportDir;
        return Path.Combine(reportParent, PortalRootFolderName);
    }

    private static void ClearDirectoryContents(string rootDir, IReadOnlyList<string> keepFolderNames)
    {
        if (!Directory.Exists(rootDir))
            return;

        foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(rootDir, "*", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly))
            File.Delete(file);

        foreach (string dir in Directory.GetDirectories(rootDir, "*", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly))
        {
            string name = Path.GetFileName(dir);
            if (keepFolderNames.Contains(name, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                continue;

            Directory.Delete(dir, recursive: true);
        }
    }

    private static string ReadAllTextSafe(string path)
    {
        try
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path, Encoding.UTF8);
        }
        catch
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path);
        }
    }

    private static string BuildHtmlPageFileName(string relativePath)
    {
        string safe = relativePath
            .Replace('\\', '_')
            .Replace('/', '_')
            .Replace(':', '_')
            .Replace(' ', '_');

        if (safe.EndsWith(".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            safe = safe[..^4];

        return safe + ".html";
    }

    private static string BuildRawHref(string relativeRawPath)
    {
        IEnumerable<string> segments = relativeRawPath
            .Replace('\\', '/')
            .Split('/', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)
            .Select(Uri.EscapeDataString);

        return "raw/" + string.Join("/", segments);
    }

    private static string BuildReportHtml(
        string displayName,
        string sourcePath,
        FileInfo info,
        string content,
        string rawHref)
    {
        string escapedName = Html(displayName);
        string escapedSource = Html(sourcePath);
        string escapedContent = Html(content);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("<!DOCTYPE html>");
        sb.AppendLine("<html lang=\"en\">");
        sb.AppendLine("<head>");
        sb.AppendLine("    <meta charset=\"utf-8\" />");
        sb.AppendLine("    <meta name=\"viewport\" content=\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1\" />");
        sb.AppendLine($"    <title>{escapedName}</title>");
        sb.AppendLine("    <style>");
        sb.AppendLine("        body {");
        sb.AppendLine("            font-family: Consolas, \"Courier New\", monospace;");
        sb.AppendLine("            background: #111;");
        sb.AppendLine("            color: #eee;");
        sb.AppendLine("            margin: 0;");
        sb.AppendLine("            padding: 32px;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        .container {");
        sb.AppendLine("            max-width: 1400px;");
        sb.AppendLine("            margin: 0 auto;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        a {");
        sb.AppendLine("            color: #6cf;");
        sb.AppendLine("            text-decoration: none;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        a:hover {");
        sb.AppendLine("            text-decoration: underline;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        .meta {");
        sb.AppendLine("            color: #bbb;");
        sb.AppendLine("            margin-bottom: 24px;");
        sb.AppendLine("            line-height: 1.7;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        pre {");
        sb.AppendLine("            white-space: pre-wrap;");
        sb.AppendLine("            word-wrap: break-word;");
        sb.AppendLine("            background: #1a1a1a;");
        sb.AppendLine("            border: 1px solid #333;");
        sb.AppendLine("            padding: 18px;");
        sb.AppendLine("            border-radius: 8px;");
        sb.AppendLine("            overflow-x: auto;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("    </style>");
        sb.AppendLine("</head>");
        sb.AppendLine("<body>");
        sb.AppendLine("    <div class=\"container\">");
        sb.AppendLine("        <div><a href=\"index.html\">← Back to index</a></div>");
        sb.AppendLine($"        <h1>{escapedName}</h1>");
        sb.AppendLine("        <div class=\"meta\">");
        sb.AppendLine($"            <div><strong>Source:</strong> {escapedSource}</div>");
        sb.AppendLine($"            <div><strong>Modified:</strong> {info.LastWriteTime:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}</div>");
        sb.AppendLine($"            <div><strong>Size:</strong> {info.Length:N0} bytes</div>");
        sb.AppendLine($"            <div><strong>Raw File:</strong> <a href=\"{rawHref}\">{escapedName}</a></div>");
        sb.AppendLine("        </div>");
        sb.AppendLine($"        <pre>{escapedContent}</pre>");
        sb.AppendLine("    </div>");
        sb.AppendLine("</body>");
        sb.AppendLine("</html>");

        return sb.ToString();
    }

    private static string BuildIndexHtml(
        string reportDir,
        string siteDir,
        IReadOnlyList<PublishedReportEntry> entries)
    {
        var rows = new StringBuilder();

        foreach (PublishedReportEntry entry in entries.OrderBy(x => x.DisplayName, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            string rawHref = BuildRawHref(entry.RelativeRawPath);
            string viewCell = entry.IsTextReport && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(entry.HtmlPageFileName)
                ? $"<a href=\"{Uri.EscapeDataString(entry.HtmlPageFileName)}\">view</a>"
                : "-";

            rows.AppendLine("                <tr>");
            rows.AppendLine($"                    <td>{Html(entry.DisplayName)}</td>");
            rows.AppendLine($"                    <td>{entry.Modified:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}</td>");
            rows.AppendLine($"                    <td style=\"text-align:right;\">{entry.SizeBytes:N0}</td>");
            rows.AppendLine($"                    <td>{viewCell}</td>");
            rows.AppendLine($"                    <td><a href=\"{rawHref}\">raw</a></td>");
            rows.AppendLine("                </tr>");
        }

        if (rows.Length == 0)
        {
            rows.AppendLine("                <tr>");
            rows.AppendLine("                    <td colspan=\"5\">No files found.</td>");
            rows.AppendLine("                </tr>");
        }

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("<!DOCTYPE html>");
        sb.AppendLine("<html lang=\"en\">");
        sb.AppendLine("<head>");
        sb.AppendLine("    <meta charset=\"utf-8\" />");
        sb.AppendLine("    <meta name=\"viewport\" content=\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1\" />");
        sb.AppendLine("    <title>TQGA Research Reports</title>");

        sb.AppendLine("            text-decoration: underline;");
        sb.AppendLine("        }");
        sb.AppendLine("        .meta {");
        sb.AppendLine("            color: #bbb;");

using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class StrategyContributionReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary<int, decimal> pnl)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 08 — STRATEGY CONTRIBUTION");
        sb.AppendLine("==================================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (pnl == null || pnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: StrategyPnL is empty.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var p in pnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"Strategy {p.Key:00} → PnL {p.Value:F2}");
        }

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(
                DataPaths.Reports,
                $"REPORT_08_STRATEGY_PNL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }
}

using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class StrategySymbolTimeframePnlReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary<string, decimal> strategySymbolTimeframePnL)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 13 — STRATEGY × SYMBOL × TIMEFRAME PnL");
        sb.AppendLine("=============================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("Key format: S##::SYMBOL::TF  (example: S02::ATOMUSDT::1h)");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (strategySymbolTimeframePnL == null || strategySymbolTimeframePnL.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("TOP 100 (by PnL)");
            sb.AppendLine("----------------");
            foreach (var kv in strategySymbolTimeframePnL.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(100))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-32} {kv.Value,14:F2}");

            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine("FULL LIST (sorted by PnL desc)");
            sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
            foreach (var kv in strategySymbolTimeframePnL.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-32} {kv.Value,14:F2}");
        }

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_13_STRATEGY_SYMBOL_TF_PNL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class StructureReportService
{
    public void Generate()
    {
        var strategyTypes = AppDomain.CurrentDomain
            .GetAssemblies()
            .SelectMany(a => a.GetTypes())
            .Where(t => typeof(IStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t)
                     && !t.IsAbstract
                     && !t.IsInterface)
            .OrderBy(t => t.Name)
            .ToList();

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA ARCHITECTURE REPORT");
        sb.AppendLine("========================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("REGISTERED STRATEGIES");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");

        int id = 1;

        foreach (var s in strategyTypes)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"[{id:00}] {s.Name}");
            id++;
        }

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports,
                $"STRUCTURE_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }
}

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class SymbolHeatmapReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary<string, decimal> pnl)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 09 — SYMBOL HEATMAP");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (pnl == null || pnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var s in pnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{s.Key,-24} {s.Value,12:F2}");
        }

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_09_SYMBOL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class SymbolTimeframePnlReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary<string, decimal> symbolTimeframePnL)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 11 — SYMBOL × TIMEFRAME PnL");
        sb.AppendLine("=================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("Key format: SYMBOL::TF  (example: ATOMUSDT::1h)");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (symbolTimeframePnL == null || symbolTimeframePnL.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("TOP 50 (by PnL)");
            sb.AppendLine("----------------");
            foreach (var kv in symbolTimeframePnL.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(50))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-24} {kv.Value,14:F2}");

            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine("FULL LIST (sorted by PnL desc)");
            sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
            foreach (var kv in symbolTimeframePnL.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-24} {kv.Value,14:F2}");
        }

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_11_SYMBOL_TF_PNL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class UniversalResearchReportService
{
    public void GenerateAll(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList<Type> selectedStrategies)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedStrategies);

        // PATCH 12 / PATCH 15:
        // One single stored canonical dictionary instance is the source of truth.
        // No fallback recompute path is allowed here.
        var canonicalCio = GetStoredCanonicalCioOrThrow(result);

        new A84MarketRegimeDetectionReportService().Generate(result);
        new A84AlphaDecayMonitoringReportService().Generate(result);

        var fitnessSvc = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService();
        var cfg = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService.FitnessConfig();

        var (fitnessRows, allowed) = fitnessSvc.ComputeFitness(result, cfg);

        // PATCH 15:
        // A84_04 scenario mode now needs full portfolio context:
        // equity timeline, canonical CIO concentration, and current run outcome.
        new A84_RegimeResearchService().Generate(
            result,
            canonicalCio);

        // A84_05
        result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights = canonicalCio;
        fitnessSvc.GenerateAndWrite(result, runUtc, cfg);

        var fitnessSnapshots = fitnessRows.ToDictionary(
            kv => kv.Key,
            kv => new StrategyFitnessSnapshot
            {
                StrategyId = kv.Value.StrategyId,
                StrategyCode = kv.Value.StrategyCode,
                PnL = kv.Value.PnL,
                Trades = kv.Value.Trades,
                Exits = kv.Value.Exits,
                FitnessScore = kv.Value.FitnessScore,
                Allowed = kv.Value.Allowed,
                GateReason = kv.Value.GateReason
            });

        // REPORT 19 — EDGE DEATH MAP
        // Must be generated inside the main universal report path so FULL REPORT / REPORT ALL 31
        // automatically includes it from DataPaths.Reports.
        new Report19EdgeDeathMapReportService().GenerateAndWrite(
            result,
            runUtc,
            fitnessSnapshots,
            allowed);

        // A84_00
        new A84ExecutiveSummaryReportService().GenerateAndWrite(
            result,
            runUtc,
            selectedStrategies,
            canonicalCio,
            recentMinutesWindow: 10);

        // A84_06
        new A84ChatGptUploadReportService().GenerateAndWrite(
            result,
            runUtc,
            selectedStrategies,
            fitnessSnapshots,
            allowed,
            canonicalCio);
    }

    private static Dictionary<string, decimal> GetStoredCanonicalCioOrThrow(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        if (result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights == null)
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "PATCH 12: Stored CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights is null.");

        if (result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "PATCH 12: Stored CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights is empty.");

        return result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights;
    }
}

using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class WalkForwardValidationReportService
{
    public void GenerateProxyReports(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList<Type> selectedStrategies)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedStrategies);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        var wf01 = Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"WF_01_SPLITS_{stamp}.txt");
        var wf02 = Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"WF_02_FOLD_SUMMARY_{stamp}.txt");
        var wf05 = Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"WF_05_WALKFORWARD_EQUITY_{stamp}.csv");
        var wf06 = Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"WF_06_CHATGPT_UPLOAD_{stamp}.txt");

        var folds = result.WalkForwardFolds
            .OrderBy(x => x.FoldNo)
            .ToList();

        if (folds.Count == 0)
        {
            File.WriteAllText(wf01, "WF_01 — SPLITS\r\n================\r\n\r\nNo walk-forward folds available.");
            File.WriteAllText(wf02, "WF_02 — FOLD SUMMARY\r\n=====================\r\n\r\nNo walk-forward folds available.");
            File.WriteAllText(wf05, "Fold,TrainStartUtc,TrainEndUtc,TestStartUtc,TestEndUtc,StartEquity,EndEquity,ReturnPct,TestPoints\r\n");
            File.WriteAllText(wf06, "WF_06 — CHATGPT UPLOAD\r\n=======================\r\n\r\nNo walk-forward folds available.");
            return;
        }

        WriteSplitReport(wf01, runUtc, selectedStrategies, folds);
        WriteFoldSummaryReport(wf02, runUtc, folds);
        WriteWalkForwardEquityCsv(wf05, folds);
        WriteCompactUpload(wf06, runUtc, selectedStrategies, folds, result);
    }

    private static void WriteSplitReport(
        string path,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList<Type> selectedStrategies,
        IReadOnlyList<WalkForwardFoldSnapshot> folds)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine("WF_01 — TRUE WALK-FORWARD SPLITS");
        sb.AppendLine("================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Selected : {selectedStrategies.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("METHOD");
        sb.AppendLine("------");
        sb.AppendLine("Rule-based walk-forward rerun.");
        sb.AppendLine("Each fold uses chronological train warmup followed by unseen test window evaluation.");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("FOLDS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----");

        foreach (var f in folds)
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"Fold {f.FoldNo:00} | TRAIN {f.TrainStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} -> {f.TrainEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} | TEST {f.TestStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} -> {f.TestEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} | TestPoints {f.TestPoints}");
        }

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteFoldSummaryReport(
        string path,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList<WalkForwardFoldSnapshot> folds)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine("WF_02 — TRUE FOLD SUMMARY");
        sb.AppendLine("=========================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("Fold | Start Equity | End Equity | Return % | Test Points");
        sb.AppendLine("-----+--------------+------------+----------+------------");

        foreach (var f in folds)
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{f.FoldNo,4} | {f.StartEquity,12:F2} | {f.EndEquity,10:F2} | {f.ReturnPct,8:F2} | {f.TestPoints,10}");
        }

        var positive = folds.Count(x => x.ReturnPct > 0m);
        var negative = folds.Count(x => x.ReturnPct < 0m);
        var stability = folds.Count == 0 ? 0m : (decimal)positive / folds.Count * 100m;

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SUMMARY");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive folds : {positive}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Negative folds : {negative}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Fold stability : {stability:F2}%");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteWalkForwardEquityCsv(
        string path,
        IReadOnlyList<WalkForwardFoldSnapshot> folds)
    {
        var lines = new List<string>
        {
            "Fold,TrainStartUtc,TrainEndUtc,TestStartUtc,TestEndUtc,StartEquity,EndEquity,ReturnPct,TestPoints"
        };

        lines.AddRange(folds.Select(f =>
            $"{f.FoldNo},{f.TrainStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss},{f.TrainEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss},{f.TestStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss},{f.TestEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss},{f.StartEquity:F2},{f.EndEquity:F2},{f.ReturnPct:F4},{f.TestPoints}"));

        File.WriteAllLines(path, lines);
    }

    private static void WriteCompactUpload(
        string path,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList<Type> selectedStrategies,
        IReadOnlyList<WalkForwardFoldSnapshot> folds,
        PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine("WF_06 — CHATGPT UPLOAD");
        sb.AppendLine("======================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Selected : {selectedStrategies.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Equity Points       : {result.PortfolioEquityTimeline.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("NOTE");
        sb.AppendLine("----");
        sb.AppendLine("True rule-based walk-forward rerun with chronological train warmup and unseen test windows.");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("FOLD RETURNS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------");

        foreach (var f in folds)
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"Fold {f.FoldNo:00} | TestReturn {f.ReturnPct:F2}% | TestPoints {f.TestPoints}");
        }

        var best = folds.OrderByDescending(x => x.ReturnPct).First();
        var worst = folds.OrderBy(x => x.ReturnPct).First();

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("EXTREMES");
        sb.AppendLine("--------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Best Fold  : F{best.FoldNo:00} {best.ReturnPct:F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Worst Fold : F{worst.FoldNo:00} {worst.ReturnPct:F2}%");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Strategy;

public sealed class DiagnosticQuantStrategy : QuantStrategy
{
    public override string Name => "Regime Pullback Quant";

    private int _ticks;

    private int _emaLong;
    private int _rsiLong;
    private int _rsiExit;

    private bool _bullishRegime;

    private int _entries;
    private int _exits;

    public override void Initialize()
    {
    }

    public override TradeSignal OnTick(StrategyContext context)
    {
        _ticks++;

        bool pullback = false;
        bool exit = false;

        foreach (var signal in Signals)
        {
            var result = signal.Evaluate(context);

            if (signal.GetType().Name == "EmaCrossSignal")
            {
                if (result == TradeSignal.Long)
                {
                    _bullishRegime = true;
                    _emaLong++;
                }
            }

            if (signal.GetType().Name == "RsiReversionSignal")
            {
                if (result == TradeSignal.Long)
                {
                    pullback = true;
                    _rsiLong++;
                }

                if (result == TradeSignal.Exit)
                {
                    exit = true;
                    _rsiExit++;
                }
            }
        }

        if (_bullishRegime && pullback && !context.HasOpenPosition)
        {
            _entries++;
            return TradeSignal.Long;
        }

        if (context.HasOpenPosition && exit)
        {
            _exits++;
            return TradeSignal.Exit;
        }

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }

    public void PrintStats()
    {
        Console.WriteLine("\n========= SIGNAL TELEMETRY =========");
        Console.WriteLine($"Ticks processed      : {_ticks}");
        Console.WriteLine($"EMA bullish signals  : {_emaLong}");
        Console.WriteLine($"RSI pullbacks        : {_rsiLong}");
        Console.WriteLine($"RSI exits            : {_rsiExit}");
        Console.WriteLine($"Entries              : {_entries}");
        Console.WriteLine($"Exits                : {_exits}");
        Console.WriteLine($"Regime active        : {_bullishRegime}");
        Console.WriteLine("====================================\n");
    }

    public void AddSignal(ISignal signal)
    {
        Signals.Add(signal);
    }
}

using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Strategy;

public abstract class QuantStrategy : IStrategy
{
    public abstract string Name { get; }

    protected readonly List<ISignal> Signals = new();

    public virtual void Initialize()
    {
    }

    // ✅ NEW — SIGNAL INJECTION SUPPORT (for StrategyFactory)
    public void SetSignals(IEnumerable<ISignal> signals)
    {
        Signals.Clear();
        Signals.AddRange(signals);
    }

    public virtual TradeSignal OnTick(StrategyContext context)
    {
        foreach (var signal in Signals)
        {
            var result = signal.Evaluate(context);

            if (result != TradeSignal.None)
                return result;
        }

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }
}

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;

namespace TQGA.Application.Strategy;

/// <summary>
/// StrategyFactory is the ONLY place responsible for instantiating concrete strategies.
/// - Uses ActivatorUtilities so DI can inject dependencies when needed.
/// - Also provides discovery of concrete IStrategy types across loaded assemblies.
/// </summary>
public sealed class StrategyFactory
{
    private readonly IServiceProvider _root;

    public StrategyFactory(IServiceProvider root)
    {
        _root = root;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Create a strategy instance of the provided type using DI.
    /// The type MUST implement IStrategy and MUST be concrete (not abstract).
    /// </summary>
    public IStrategy Create(Type strategyType)
    {
        if (strategyType is null)
            throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategyType));

        if (!typeof(IStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(strategyType))
            throw new ArgumentException($"Type '{strategyType.FullName}' does not implement IStrategy.");

        if (strategyType.IsAbstract || strategyType.IsInterface)
            throw new ArgumentException($"Type '{strategyType.FullName}' is abstract/interface and cannot be created.");

        var instance = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance(_root, strategyType);

        if (instance is not IStrategy strategy)
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"Activator created '{strategyType.FullName}' but it is not IStrategy.");

        return strategy;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Discovers all concrete IStrategy types from currently loaded assemblies.
    /// This avoids Application referencing Infrastructure directly.
    /// </summary>
    public static IReadOnlyList<Type> DiscoverConcreteStrategyTypes()
    {
        var types =
            AppDomain.CurrentDomain
                .GetAssemblies()
                .SelectMany(a =>
                {
                    try { return a.GetTypes(); }
                    catch { return Array.Empty<Type>(); }
                })
                .Where(t =>
                    t is not null &&
                    typeof(IStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t) &&
                    !t.IsAbstract &&
                    !t.IsInterface)
                .Distinct()
                .OrderBy(t => t.Name)
                .ToList();

        return types;
    }
}

using System.Text;
using System.Threading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Trading;

public sealed class TradeDecisionDiagnostics
{
    // ================= INTERNAL COUNTERS =================

    private int _ticksProcessed;
    private int _signalLong;
    private int _signalShort;
    private int _signalExit;
    private int _entryAttempts;
    private int _executedEntries;
    private int _executedExits;

    // ================= PUBLIC READ MODEL =================

    public int TicksProcessed => _ticksProcessed;
    public int SignalLong => _signalLong;
    public int SignalShort => _signalShort;
    public int SignalExit => _signalExit;
    public int EntryAttempts => _entryAttempts;
    public int ExecutedEntries => _executedEntries;
    public int ExecutedExits => _executedExits;

    // ================= ENGINE WRITE API =================

    public void OnTickProcessed() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _ticksProcessed);
    public void OnSignalLong() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalLong);
    public void OnSignalShort() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalShort);
    public void OnSignalExit() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalExit);

    public void OnEntryAttempt() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _entryAttempts);
    public void OnEntryExecuted() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _executedEntries);
    public void OnExitExecuted() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _executedExits);

    public void Reset()
    {
        _ticksProcessed = 0;
        _signalLong = 0;
        _signalShort = 0;
        _signalExit = 0;
        _entryAttempts = 0;
        _executedEntries = 0;
        _executedExits = 0;
    }

    // ================= REPORT BUILDER =================

    public string BuildReport()
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("EXECUTION ATTRIBUTION");
        sb.AppendLine("=====================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine($"Ticks processed           : {TicksProcessed}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Signal LONG               : {SignalLong}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Signal SHORT              : {SignalShort}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Signal EXIT               : {SignalExit}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Entry attempts            : {EntryAttempts}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Executed Entries          : {ExecutedEntries}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Executed Exits            : {ExecutedExits}");

        return sb.ToString();
    }
}

namespace TQGA.Application.Trading;

public sealed record TradeResult(
    DateTime Time,
    decimal TradePnL,
    decimal Equity,
    decimal Drawdown);

using TQGA.Application.Accounting;
using TQGA.Application.Risk;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Trading;

public sealed class TradingEngine : ITradingEngine
{
    private readonly IStrategy _strategy;
    private readonly IOrderExecutor _executor;
    private readonly TradeLedger _ledger;
    private readonly EquityCurve _equity;
    private readonly ICapitalAllocator _capital;
    private readonly IRiskManager _risk;
    private readonly TradeDecisionDiagnostics _diag;

    private Trade? _openTrade;

    public TradingEngine(
        IStrategy strategy,
        IOrderExecutor executor,
        TradeLedger ledger,
        EquityCurve equity,
        ICapitalAllocator capital,
        IRiskManager risk,
        TradeDecisionDiagnostics diag)
    {
        _strategy = strategy;
        _executor = executor;
        _ledger = ledger;
        _equity = equity;
        _capital = capital;
        _risk = risk;
        _diag = diag;
    }

    public async Task OnTickAsync(
        string symbol,
        decimal price,
        DateTime time,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        // Market sync (executor uses last price as fill in backtests)
        _executor.UpdateMarketPrice(price);
        _diag.OnTickProcessed();

        // Mark-to-market equity update
        if (_openTrade != null)
        {
            var unrealized =
                (_openTrade.Side == TradeSide.Buy
                    ? price - _openTrade.EntryPrice
                    : _openTrade.EntryPrice - price)
                * _openTrade.Quantity;

            _equity.Update(time, _capital.CurrentEquity + unrealized);
        }
        else
        {
            _equity.Update(time, _capital.CurrentEquity);
        }

        // Strategy decision
        var context = new StrategyContext(
            price,
            time,
            _openTrade != null,
            _openTrade?.Quantity ?? 0m);

        var signal = _strategy.OnTick(context);

        // ========= ENTRY (LONG) =========
        if (signal == TradeSignal.Long)
        {
            _diag.OnSignalLong();

            if (_openTrade != null) return;
            if (!_risk.CanContinueTrading()) return;

            var size = _capital.GetOrderSize(symbol, price);
            if (size <= 0m) return;

            if (!_risk.CanEnterPosition(size)) return;

            _diag.OnEntryAttempt();

            await _executor.PlaceMarketOrderAsync(
                symbol,
                TradeSide.Buy,
                size,
                ct);

            var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice();

            _openTrade = new Trade(
                symbol,
                TradeSide.Buy,
                size,
                fillPrice,
                time);

            _diag.OnEntryExecuted();
            return;
        }

        // ========= ENTRY (SHORT) =========
        if (signal == TradeSignal.Short)
        {
            _diag.OnSignalShort();

            if (_openTrade != null) return;
            if (!_risk.CanContinueTrading()) return;

            var size = _capital.GetOrderSize(symbol, price);
            if (size <= 0m) return;

            if (!_risk.CanEnterPosition(size)) return;

            _diag.OnEntryAttempt();

            await _executor.PlaceMarketOrderAsync(
                symbol,
                TradeSide.Sell,
                size,
                ct);

            var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice();

            _openTrade = new Trade(
                symbol,
                TradeSide.Sell,
                size,
                fillPrice,
                time);

            _diag.OnEntryExecuted();
            return;
        }

        // ========= EXIT =========
        if (signal == TradeSignal.Exit)
        {
            _diag.OnSignalExit();

            if (_openTrade == null) return;

            await _executor.ClosePositionAsync(symbol, ct);

            var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice();

            _openTrade.Close(fillPrice, time);

            // Bookkeeping
            _ledger.Record(_openTrade);
            _capital.OnTradeClosed(_openTrade.RealizedPnL);
            _risk.OnTradeClosed(_openTrade.RealizedPnL);

            _diag.OnExitExecuted();

            _openTrade = null;
            return;
        }
    }
}

namespace TQGA.Domain.Indicators;

public sealed class Ema : IIndicator
{
    private readonly decimal _alpha;
    private decimal? _ema;

    public Ema(int period)
    {
        _alpha = 2m / (period + 1);
    }

    public void Add(decimal value)
    {
        _ema = _ema == null
            ? value
            : value * _alpha + _ema.Value * (1 - _alpha);
    }

    public decimal Value => _ema ?? 0m;

    public bool IsReady => _ema.HasValue;
}

namespace TQGA.Domain.Indicators;

public sealed class Rsi
{
    private readonly int _period;

    private decimal _avgGain;
    private decimal _avgLoss;

    private decimal? _previousPrice;
    private int _samples;

    public bool IsReady => _samples >= _period;
    public decimal Value { get; private set; }

    public Rsi(int period)
    {
        if (period <= 0)
            throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(period));

        _period = period;
    }

    public void Update(decimal price)
    {
        if (_previousPrice == null)
        {
            _previousPrice = price;
            return;
        }

        var change = price - _previousPrice.Value;
        var gain = change > 0 ? change : 0;
        var loss = change < 0 ? -change : 0;

        if (_samples < _period)
        {
            _avgGain += gain;
            _avgLoss += loss;
            _samples++;

            if (_samples == _period)
            {
                _avgGain /= _period;
                _avgLoss /= _period;
                CalculateRsi();
            }
        }
        else
        {
            _avgGain = (_avgGain * (_period - 1) + gain) / _period;
            _avgLoss = (_avgLoss * (_period - 1) + loss) / _period;

            CalculateRsi();
        }

        _previousPrice = price;
    }

    private void CalculateRsi()
    {
        if (_avgLoss == 0)
        {
            Value = 100;
            return;
        }

        var rs = _avgGain / _avgLoss;
        Value = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs));
    }

    public void Reset()
    {
        _avgGain = 0;
        _avgLoss = 0;
        _previousPrice = null;
        _samples = 0;
        Value = 0;
    }
}

public sealed class Position
{

    {

namespace TQGA.Domain.Trading;

public sealed class Trade
{
    public string Symbol { get; }
    public TradeSide Side { get; }
    public decimal Quantity { get; }
    public decimal EntryPrice { get; }
    public DateTime EntryTime { get; }

    public decimal? ExitPrice { get; private set; }
    public DateTime? ExitTime { get; private set; }

    public bool IsClosed => ExitPrice.HasValue;

    public Trade(
        string symbol,
        TradeSide side,
        decimal quantity,
        decimal entryPrice,
        DateTime entryTime)
    {
        Symbol = symbol;
        Side = side;
        Quantity = quantity;
        EntryPrice = entryPrice;
        EntryTime = entryTime;
    }

    public void Close(decimal exitPrice, DateTime exitTime)
    {
        ExitPrice = exitPrice;
        ExitTime = exitTime;
    }

    public decimal RealizedPnL =>
        !IsClosed
            ? 0m
            : Side == TradeSide.Buy
                ? (ExitPrice!.Value - EntryPrice) * Quantity
                : (EntryPrice - ExitPrice!.Value) * Quantity;
}

using System.Globalization;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Data;

public sealed class CandleDataCleaner
{
    private readonly string _candlesRoot;

    public CandleDataCleaner(string candlesRoot)
    {
        _candlesRoot = candlesRoot;
    }

    public void Run()
    {
        var files = Directory.GetFiles(_candlesRoot, "*.csv");

        foreach (var file in files)
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"\n🧹 CLEANING: {Path.GetFileName(file)}");

            Backup(file);

            var cleaned = CleanFile(file);

            File.WriteAllLines(file, cleaned);

            Console.WriteLine("✅ DONE");
        }
    }

    private static void Backup(string file)
    {
        var backup = file + ".bak";

        File.Copy(file, backup, true);

        Console.WriteLine("📦 Backup created");
    }

    private static List<string> CleanFile(string file)
    {
        var lines = File.ReadAllLines(file).ToList();

        var header = lines.First();

        var candles = lines
            .Skip(1)
            .Select(Parse)
            .Where(x => x != null)
            .Select(x => x!)
            .ToList();

        // SORT
        candles = candles
            .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
            .ToList();

        // REMOVE DUPLICATES
        candles = candles
            .GroupBy(c => c.Time)
            .Select(g => g.First())
            .ToList();

        // CHECK CONTINUITY
        ValidateContinuity(candles);

        // REBUILD
        var output = new List<string> { header };

        output.AddRange(candles.Select(ToCsv));

        return output;
    }

    private static CandleRow? Parse(string line)
    {
        var p = line.Split(',');

        if (p.Length < 6)
            return null;

        return new CandleRow
        {
            Time = DateTime.Parse(p[0], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
            Open = p[1],
            High = p[2],
            Low = p[3],
            Close = p[4],
            Volume = p[5]
        };
    }

    private static string ToCsv(CandleRow c)
    {
        return string.Join(",",
            c.Time.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"),
            c.Open,
            c.High,
            c.Low,
            c.Close,
            c.Volume);
    }

    private static void ValidateContinuity(List<CandleRow> candles)
    {
        var expectedStep = TimeSpan.FromHours(1);

        for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++)
        {
            var diff = candles[i].Time - candles[i - 1].Time;

            if (diff != expectedStep)
            {
                Console.WriteLine(
                    $"⚠ GAP or overlap: {candles[i - 1].Time} → {candles[i].Time}  ({diff})");
            }
        }
    }

    private sealed class CandleRow
    {
        public DateTime Time { get; set; }
        public string Open { get; set; } = "";
        public string High { get; set; } = "";
        public string Low { get; set; } = "";
        public string Close { get; set; } = "";
        public string Volume { get; set; } = "";
    }
}

using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using TQGA.Application.Accounting;
using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;
using TQGA.Application.Risk;
using TQGA.Application.Trading;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.Risk;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure;

public static class DependencyInjection
{
    public static IServiceCollection AddInfrastructure(this IServiceCollection services)
    {
        // Market data
        services.AddSingleton<ICandleDataFeed, CsvCandleDataFeed>();

        // Bootstrapper used by WinForms buttons
        services.AddSingleton<HistoricalDataBootstrapper>();

        // Trading stack required by BacktestRunner / PortfolioBacktestRunner / TradingEngine
        services.AddScoped<ITradingEngine, TradingEngine>();
        services.AddScoped<IOrderExecutor, BacktestOrderExecutor>();
        services.AddScoped<IRiskManager, SimpleRiskManager>();
        services.AddScoped<ICapitalAllocator, StrategyCapitalAllocator>();

        // Per-run stateful accounting / diagnostics services
        services.AddScoped<TradeLedger>();
        services.AddScoped<EquityCurve>();
        services.AddScoped<TradeDecisionDiagnostics>();

        return services;
    }
}

using System.Globalization;
using System.Net.Http;
using System.Text.Json;
using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

public sealed class BinanceDownloader
{
    private static readonly HttpClient _http = new()
    {
        BaseAddress = new Uri("https://api.binance.com")
    };

    private const int LimitPerRequest = 1000;

    public async Task<List<Candle>> DownloadAsync(
        string symbol,
        string interval,
        DateTime startUtc,
        DateTime endUtc,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        var candles = new List<Candle>();

        long startMs = ToUnixMs(startUtc);
        long endMs = ToUnixMs(endUtc);

        while (startMs < endMs)
        {
            var url =
                $"/api/v3/klines?symbol={symbol}" +
                $"&interval={interval}" +
                $"&startTime={startMs}" +
                $"&endTime={endMs}" +
                $"&limit={LimitPerRequest}";

            var response = await _http.GetAsync(url, ct);
            response.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();

            var json = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync(ct);
            var data = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<List<List<JsonElement>>>(json);

            if (data == null || data.Count == 0)
                break;

            foreach (var item in data)
            {
                var openTime = DateTimeOffset
                    .FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(item[0].GetInt64())
                    .UtcDateTime;

                candles.Add(new Candle(
                    openTime,
                    decimal.Parse(item[1].GetString()!, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                    decimal.Parse(item[2].GetString()!, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                    decimal.Parse(item[3].GetString()!, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                    decimal.Parse(item[4].GetString()!, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                    decimal.Parse(item[5].GetString()!, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)
                ));
            }

            startMs = data.Last()[0].GetInt64() + 1;

            await Task.Delay(300, ct); // rate-limit safe
        }

        return candles;
    }

    private static long ToUnixMs(DateTime dt)
        => new DateTimeOffset(dt).ToUnixTimeMilliseconds();
}

using System.Net.Http.Json;
using System.Text.Json;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Data;

public sealed class BinanceDownloaderService
{
    private readonly HttpClient _http = new();
    private readonly BinanceRateLimiter _rateLimiter = new();
    private readonly CandleFileWriter _writer = new();

    public async Task IncrementalUpdateAsync(
        string symbol,
        string interval,
        IProgress<int>? progress,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        var last = _writer.GetLastCandleTime(symbol, interval);

        DateTime start =
            last?.AddHours(1) ??
            DateTime.UtcNow.AddYears(-5);

        DateTime end = DateTime.UtcNow;

        var allCandles = new List<string>();

        int batch = 0;

        while (start < end)
        {
            await _rateLimiter.WaitAsync(ct);

            var url =
                $"https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines" +
                $"?symbol={symbol}" +
                $"&interval={interval}" +
                $"&startTime={new DateTimeOffset(start).ToUnixTimeMilliseconds()}" +
                $"&limit=1000";

            var data = await RetryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(async () =>
                await _http.GetStringAsync(url, ct));

            var json = JsonDocument.Parse(data);

            if (json.RootElement.GetArrayLength() == 0)
                break;

            foreach (var item in json.RootElement.EnumerateArray())
            {
                var line =
                    $"{DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(item[0].GetInt64()).UtcDateTime:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm}," +
                    $"{item[1]}," +
                    $"{item[2]}," +
                    $"{item[3]}," +
                    $"{item[4]}," +
                    $"{item[5]}";

                allCandles.Add(line);
            }

            // JsonElement does not support the C# Index (^) operator on its indexer,
            // so compute the last index explicitly.
            var arrLen = json.RootElement.GetArrayLength();
            if (arrLen == 0)
                break;

            start = DateTimeOffset
                .FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(
                    json.RootElement[arrLen - 1][0].GetInt64())
                .UtcDateTime
                .AddHours(1);

            batch++;
            progress?.Report(batch);
        }

        _writer.AppendOrCreate(symbol, interval, allCandles);
    }
}

using System.Threading;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Data;

public sealed class BinanceRateLimiter
{
    private readonly SemaphoreSlim _semaphore = new(1, 1);
    private DateTime _lastCall = DateTime.MinValue;

    private const int MinDelayMs = 250; // 4 calls per second max

    public async Task WaitAsync(CancellationToken ct)
    {
        await _semaphore.WaitAsync(ct);

        try
        {
            var elapsed = DateTime.UtcNow - _lastCall;

            if (elapsed.TotalMilliseconds < MinDelayMs)
            {
                var delay = MinDelayMs - (int)elapsed.TotalMilliseconds;
                await Task.Delay(delay, ct);
            }

            _lastCall = DateTime.UtcNow;
        }
        finally
        {
            _semaphore.Release();
        }
    }
}

using System.Globalization;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

public sealed class CandleFileWriter
{
    private static readonly string BasePath = DataPaths.Candles;
    private static string GetPath(string symbol, string interval)
        => Path.Combine(BasePath, $"{symbol}_{interval}.csv");

    public DateTime? GetLastCandleTime(string symbol, string interval)
    {
        var path = GetPath(symbol, interval);

        if (!File.Exists(path))
            return null;

        var lastLine = File.ReadLines(path).LastOrDefault();

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(lastLine))
            return null;

        var parts = lastLine.Split(',');

        return DateTime.Parse(parts[0], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
    }

    public void AppendOrCreate(
        string symbol,
        string interval,
        IEnumerable<CandleDto> candles)
    {
        var path = GetPath(symbol, interval);

        var exists = File.Exists(path);

        using var writer = new StreamWriter(path, append: true);

        if (!exists)
        {
            writer.WriteLine("Time,Open,High,Low,Close,Volume");
        }

        foreach (var c in candles)
        {
            writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",",
                c.Time.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"),
                c.Open.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                c.High.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                c.Low.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                c.Close.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                c.Volume.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)
            ));
        }
    }

    // Overload to accept preformatted CSV lines (used by downloader service)
    public void AppendOrCreate(
        string symbol,
        string interval,
        IEnumerable<string> csvLines)
    {
        var path = GetPath(symbol, interval);

        var exists = File.Exists(path);

        using var writer = new StreamWriter(path, append: true);

        if (!exists)
        {
            writer.WriteLine("Time,Open,High,Low,Close,Volume");
        }

        foreach (var line in csvLines)
        {
            writer.WriteLine(line);
        }
    }
}

public sealed class CandleDto
{
    public DateTime Time { get; init; }
    public decimal Open { get; init; }
    public decimal High { get; init; }
    public decimal Low { get; init; }
    public decimal Close { get; init; }
    public decimal Volume { get; init; }
}

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Globalization;
using System.IO;
using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

/// <summary>
/// Reads candles from CSV files stored at:
/// DataPaths.Candles\{SYMBOL}_{TF}.csv
/// Example: BTCUSDT_1h.csv
/// CSV expected columns: Time,Open,High,Low,Close,Volume
/// </summary>
public sealed class CsvCandleDataFeed : ICandleDataFeed
{
    private readonly string _root;

    public CsvCandleDataFeed()
    {
        _root = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(DataPaths.Candles)
            ? Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "MarketData", "Candles")
            : DataPaths.Candles;
    }

    public IEnumerable<Candle> GetCandles(string symbol, string timeframe)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol))
            throw new ArgumentException("Symbol is required.", nameof(symbol));

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(timeframe))
            throw new ArgumentException("Timeframe is required.", nameof(timeframe));

        var file = Path.Combine(_root, $"{symbol}_{timeframe}.csv");

        if (!File.Exists(file))
            throw new FileNotFoundException($"Candle file not found: {file}");

        foreach (var line in File.ReadLines(file))
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(line))
                continue;

            // Skip header lines safely
            if (line.StartsWith("Time", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                line.StartsWith("Open", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                continue;

            var parts = line.Split(',', StringSplitOptions.TrimEntries);
            if (parts.Length < 6)
                continue;

            if (!TryParseTime(parts[0], out var t))
                continue;

            if (!TryDec(parts[1], out var o)) continue;
            if (!TryDec(parts[2], out var h)) continue;
            if (!TryDec(parts[3], out var l)) continue;
            if (!TryDec(parts[4], out var c)) continue;

            // Volume sometimes missing/blank in some CSVs -> default to 0
            decimal v = 0m;
            _ = TryDec(parts[5], out v);

            // ✅ Candle is immutable in your Domain: construct via ctor
            yield return new Candle(t, o, h, l, c, v);
        }
    }

    private static bool TryDec(string s, out decimal d)
        => decimal.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Any, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out d);

    private static bool TryParseTime(string raw, out DateTime t)
    {
        raw = raw.Trim();

        // Unix ms or unix sec
        if (long.TryParse(raw, out var n))
        {
            if (n > 1_000_000_000_000) // ms
            {
                t = DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(n).UtcDateTime;
                return true;
            }

            if (n > 1_000_000_000) // sec
            {
                t = DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeSeconds(n).UtcDateTime;
                return true;
            }
        }

        // ISO time
        if (DateTime.TryParse(
                raw,
                CultureInfo.InvariantCulture,
                DateTimeStyles.AssumeUniversal | DateTimeStyles.AdjustToUniversal,
                out t))
        {
            t = DateTime.SpecifyKind(t, DateTimeKind.Utc);
            return true;
        }

        t = default;
        return false;
    }
}

using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

public sealed class CsvMarketDataFeed : IMarketDataFeed
{
    private readonly List<decimal> _prices = new();
    private int _index;

    public CsvMarketDataFeed(string filePath)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(filePath))
            throw new FileNotFoundException(
                $"Market data file not found: {filePath}");

        _prices = File.ReadAllLines(filePath)
            .Skip(1)
            .Select(l => decimal.Parse(l.Split(',')[4]))
            .ToList();
    }

    public decimal GetLastPrice(string symbol)
    {
        if (_index >= _prices.Count)
            return _prices.Last();

        return _prices[_index++];
    }
}

using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

public sealed class HistoricalDataBootstrapper
{
    private const int FullHistoryYears = 10;

    private readonly BinanceDownloader _downloader = new();
    private readonly CandleFileWriter _writer = new();

    public Task ForceFullDownloadAsync()
        => EnsureAsync(force: true);

    public Task UpdateAsync()
        => EnsureAsync(force: false);

    public async Task EnsureAsync(bool force = false)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Candles);

        foreach (var symbol in BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols)
        {
            foreach (var tf in BinanceUniverse.Timeframes)
            {
                var path = Path.Combine(
                    DataPaths.Candles,
                    $"{symbol}_{tf}.csv");

                DateTime startUtc;

                if (!force && File.Exists(path))
                {
                    var last = _writer.GetLastCandleTime(symbol, tf);

                    startUtc = last != null
                        ? last.Value.Add(GetTimeframeStep(tf))
                        : DateTime.UtcNow.AddYears(-FullHistoryYears);
                }
                else
                {
                    startUtc = DateTime.UtcNow.AddYears(-FullHistoryYears);
                }

                if (startUtc >= DateTime.UtcNow)
                    continue;

                var candles = await _downloader.DownloadAsync(
                    symbol,
                    tf,
                    startUtc,
                    DateTime.UtcNow,
                    CancellationToken.None);

                var dtos = candles.Select(c => new CandleDto
                {
                    Time = c.Time,
                    Open = c.Open,
                    High = c.High,
                    Low = c.Low,
                    Close = c.Close,
                    Volume = c.Volume
                });

                _writer.AppendOrCreate(symbol, tf, dtos);
            }
        }
    }

    private static TimeSpan GetTimeframeStep(string tf)
    {
        return tf switch
        {
            "1h" => TimeSpan.FromHours(1),
            "4h" => TimeSpan.FromHours(4),
            "1d" => TimeSpan.FromDays(1),
            _ => TimeSpan.FromHours(1)
        };
    }
}

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Data;

public static class RetryPolicy
{
    public static async Task<T> ExecuteAsync<T>(
        Func<Task<T>> action,
        int maxAttempts = 5)
    {
        int attempt = 0;

        while (true)
        {
            try
            {
                return await action();
            }
            catch when (attempt < maxAttempts)
            {
                attempt++;
                var delay = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(Math.Pow(2, attempt));
                await Task.Delay(delay);
            }
        }
    }
}
